## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    App[platform-load-balancer Application]
    App -->|reads from| Repo[GitLab Repository]
    App -->|deploys to| Cluster[Kubernetes Cluster]
    Repo -->|contains| Helm[Helm Chart]
    Helm -->|configured by| Values[values.yaml + parameters]
    Values -->|creates| LB[Load Balancer]
    LB -->|routes| Host1[k8s.env.freightverify.com]
    LB -->|routes| Host2[k8s-deploy.env.freightverify.com]
    LB -->|routes| Host3[api.freightverify.com]
    Cluster -->|namespace| NS[default]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Application {
        +String name
        +String environment
        +Destination destination
        +Source source
        +String project
        +SyncPolicy syncPolicy
    }
    class Destination {
        +String namespace
        +String server
    }
    class Source {
        +String path
        +String repoURL
        +String targetRevision
        +Helm helm
    }
    class Helm {
        +Array valueFiles
        +Array parameters
    }
    class Parameter {
        +String name
        +String value
    }
    class SyncPolicy {
        +Object automated
        +Array syncOptions
    }
    Application --> Destination
    Application --> Source
    Application --> SyncPolicy
    Source --> Helm
    Helm --> Parameter
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Configured: Application Created
    Configured --> Syncing: Auto Sync Triggered
    Syncing --> FetchingSource: Get Helm Chart
    FetchingSource --> RenderingHelm: Apply Parameters
    RenderingHelm --> DeployingResources: Create K8s Resources
    DeployingResources --> CreatingNamespace: Ensure Namespace Exists
    CreatingNamespace --> DeployingIngress: Deploy Load Balancer
    DeployingIngress --> Healthy: All Resources Ready
    Healthy --> Syncing: Configuration Change
    Healthy --> [*]: Application Deleted
```
